\subsection{Detailed Description}
Web\+Kit main smart object. 

This object allows the high level access to Web\+Kit-\/\+E\+F\+L component. It is responsible for managing the main frame and other critical resources.

Every ewk\+\_\+view has at least one frame, called \char`\"{}main frame\char`\"{} and retrieved with \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_af21210605d1aea14d06a507854b10e3b}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+frame\+\_\+main\+\_\+get()}. Direct frame access is often discouraged, it is recommended to use ewk\+\_\+view functions instead.

The following signals (see evas\+\_\+object\+\_\+smart\+\_\+callback\+\_\+add()) are emitted\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}colorchooser,create\char`\"{}, Ewk\+\_\+\+Color\+: a new color chooser should be created.
\item \char`\"{}colorchooser,willdelete\char`\"{}, void\+: reports that a previously created color chooser will be deleted.
\item \char`\"{}colorchooser,color,changed\char`\"{}, Ewk\+\_\+\+Color\+: the value at the color input widget corresponding to the color chooser has changed.
\item \char`\"{}download,request\char`\"{}, Ewk\+\_\+\+Download\+: reports a download is being requested
\item \char`\"{}editorclient,contents,changed\char`\"{}, void\+: reports to the view that editor client's contents were changed
\item \char`\"{}frame,created\char`\"{}, Evas\+\_\+\+Object$\ast$\+: a new frame is created.
\item \char`\"{}icon,received\char`\"{}, void\+: main frame received an icon.
\item \char`\"{}inputmethod,changed\char`\"{}, Eina\+\_\+\+Bool\+: reports that input method was changed and it gives a boolean value whether it's enabled or not as an argument.
\item \char`\"{}inspector,view,close\char`\"{}, Evas\+\_\+\+Object$\ast$\+: request to close the view for inspector.
\item \char`\"{}inspector,view,create\char`\"{}, void\+: request to create the new view for inspector.
\item \char`\"{}js,windowobject,clear\char`\"{}, void\+: Report that the J\+S window object has been cleared.

Initializes to zero a whole {\itshape Ewk\+\_\+\+View\+\_\+\+Smart\+\_\+\+Class} structure and sets the name and version.

Similar to {\itshape E\+W\+K\+\_\+\+V\+I\+E\+W\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+L\+L}, but it sets the version field of {\itshape Evas\+\_\+\+Smart\+\_\+\+Class} (base field) to latest {\itshape E\+V\+A\+S\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+R\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+A\+S\+S\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N} and the name to the specific value.

It will keep a reference to the name field as a \char`\"{}const char $\ast$\char`\"{}, that is, name must be available while the structure is used (hint\+: static or global!) and it will not be modified.

\subsection{Function Documentation}
\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_af8ef52dca7685280ad63f267101cbb01}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Evas\+\_\+\+Object$\ast$ ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+add (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas $\ast$}]{e}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_af8ef52dca7685280ad63f267101cbb01}
Creates a new E\+F\+L Web\+Kit View object.

View objects are the recommended way to deal with E\+F\+L Web\+Kit as it abstracts the complex pieces of the process.

Each view is composed by a set of frames. The set has at least one frame, called 'main\+\_\+frame'. See \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_af21210605d1aea14d06a507854b10e3b}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+frame\+\_\+main\+\_\+get()} and \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a80c0f796609220d152a4621c51fca07d}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+frame\+\_\+focused\+\_\+get()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em e} & canvas object where to create the view object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
view object on success or {\ttfamily N\+U\+L\+L} on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the background color of the view.

Just as in Evas, colors are pre-\/multiplied, so 50\% red is (128, 0, 0, 128) and not (255, 0, 0, 128)!

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a2f704e8453ca4102afdb500cdbe84742}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I void ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+bg\+\_\+color\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{int}]{r, }
\item[{int}]{g, }
\item[{int}]{b, }
\item[{int}]{a}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a2f704e8453ca4102afdb500cdbe84742}
Sets the background color and transparency of the view.

Just as in Evas, colors are pre-\/multiplied, so 50\% red is (128, 0, 0, 128) and not (255, 0, 0, 128)!

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Watch out performance issues with transparency! Object will be handled as transparent image by evas even if the webpage specifies a background color. That mean you'll pay a price even if it's not really transparent, thus scrolling/panning and zooming will be likely slower than if transparency is off.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\hline
{\em a} & transparency \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Changes the color selected in the color input widget. The browser should call this when the user chooses a new color. It's likely that ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+color\+\_\+chooser\+\_\+destroy will be called afterwards.

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_aa5f43cd49c2b2d310e0566e375f7dc46}
Destroys a previously created color chooser.

Before destroying, it informs client that color chooser's data is ready to be destroyed by sending a \char`\"{}colorchooser,willdelete\char`\"{}. Then it removes any reference to the color chooser inside webkit. It's safe to call this function either from inside webkit or from browser.

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a829b24ac53544da0aa31787dab6818d3}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I float ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+device\+\_\+pixel\+\_\+ratio\+\_\+get (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a829b24ac53544da0aa31787dab6818d3}
Queries the ratio between the C\+S\+S units and device pixels when the content is unscaled.

When designing touch-\/friendly contents, knowing the approximated target size on a device is important for contents providers in order to get the intented layout and element sizes.

As most first generation touch devices had a P\+P\+I of approximately 160, this became a de-\/facto value, when used in conjunction with the viewport meta tag.

Devices with a higher P\+P\+I learning towards 240 or 320, applies a pre-\/scaling on all content, of either 1.\+5 or 2.\+0, not affecting the C\+S\+S scale or pinch zooming.

This value can be set using this property and it is exposed to C\+S\+S media queries using the -\/webkit-\/device-\/pixel-\/ratio query.

For instance, if you want to load an image without having it upscaled on a web view using a device pixel ratio of 2.\+0 it can be done by loading an image of say 100x100 pixels but showing it at half the size.

(-\/webkit-\/min-\/device-\/pixel-\/ratio\+: 1.\+5) \{ .icon \{ width\+: 50px; height\+: 50px; url\+: \char`\"{}/images/icon@2x.\+png\char`\"{}; // This is actually a 100x100 image \} \}

If the above is used on a device with device pixel ratio of 1.\+5, it will be scaled down but still provide a better looking image.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to get device pixel ratio\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the ratio between the C\+S\+S units and device pixels, or {\ttfamily -\/1.\+0} on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_ac86f6218bdf66a913c3aca8579f80500}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+layout\+\_\+size\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+layout\+\_\+size\+\_\+set}}

\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+layout\+\_\+size\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I void ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+fixed\+\_\+layout\+\_\+size\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{w, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{h}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_ac86f6218bdf66a913c3aca8579f80500}
Sets a fixed layout size to be used, dissociating it from viewport size.

Setting a width different than zero enables fixed layout on that size. It's automatically scaled based on zoom, but will not change if viewport changes.

Setting both {\itshape w} and {\itshape h} to zero will disable fixed layout.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to change fixed layout \\
\hline
{\em w} & fixed width to use, this size will be automatically scaled based on zoom level \\
\hline
{\em h} & fixed height to use, this size will be automatically scaled based on zoom level \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+history\+\_\+get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I {\bf Ewk\+\_\+\+History}$\ast$ ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+history\+\_\+get (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_ab959edecef54489989a730a58a849889}
Gets the history (back-\/forward list) associated with this view.

The returned instance is unique for this view and thus multiple calls to this function with the same view as parameter returns the same handle. This handle is alive while view is alive, thus one might want to listen for E\+V\+A\+S\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L on given view ({\itshape o}) to know when to stop using returned handle.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to get navigation history\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the history instance handle associated with this view on succes or {\ttfamily N\+U\+L\+L} on failure (including when the history navigation is not enabled with \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a60903cd4f17408d2aca97db37926a2d5}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+history\+\_\+enable\+\_\+set()})
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a22cb6fe18980039f11d265e90c621f05}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I void ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+show (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a22cb6fe18980039f11d265e90c621f05}
Show the inspector to debug a web page.

The following signals are emiited. \char`\"{}inspector,view,create\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}inspector,view,close\char`\"{} The first one will be called to request the view for inspector on view that will be inspected. This callback should create the view for inspector and set the view with \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_ac465403ce19982eeafdb4ff221fdba5e}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+view\+\_\+set()}. The second one will be called to close the view for inspector on view having the inspector after disconnecting frontend This callback should remove the view for inspector.

When the view having the inspector is removed, please emit the \char`\"{}inspector,view,destroy\char`\"{} signal on view for inspector.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & The view to show the inspector.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_af245f378dc9f1970b30e4c2487168d4a}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+close()} 

\hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_ac465403ce19982eeafdb4ff221fdba5e}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+inspector\+\_\+view\+\_\+set()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_ae025264304d5b27de66be117bb7146a2}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+mixed\+\_\+content\+\_\+displayed\+\_\+get (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_ae025264304d5b27de66be117bb7146a2}
Returns whether the view has displayed mixed content.

When a view has displayed mixed content, any of its frames has loaded an H\+T\+T\+P\+S U\+R\+I which has itself loaded and displayed a resource (such as an image) from an insecure, that is, non-\/\+H\+T\+T\+P\+S, U\+R\+I.

The status is reset only when a load event occurs (eg. the page is reloaded or a new page is loaded).

When one of the containing frames displays mixed content, the view emits the \char`\"{}mixedcontent,displayed\char`\"{} signal.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & The view to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Returns whether the view has run mixed content.

When a view has run mixed content, any of its frames has loaded an H\+T\+T\+P\+S U\+R\+I which has itself loaded and run a resource (such as an image) from an insecure, that is, non-\/\+H\+T\+T\+P\+S, U\+R\+I.

The status is reset only when a load event occurs (eg. the page is reloaded or a new page is loaded).

When one of the containing frames runs mixed content, the view emits the \char`\"{}mixedcontent,run\char`\"{} signal.

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a791459703a2443aa7a4df0e56b5ca205}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+popup\+\_\+destroy@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+popup\+\_\+destroy}}

\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+popup\+\_\+destroy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+popup\+\_\+destroy (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a791459703a2443aa7a4df0e56b5ca205}
Destroys a previously created menu.

Before destroying, it informs client that menu's data is ready to be destroyed by sending a \char`\"{}popup,willdelete\char`\"{} with a list of menu items. Then it removes any reference to menu inside webkit. It's safe to call this function either from inside webkit or from browser.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} in case menu was successfully destroyed or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} in case there wasn't any menu to be destroyed 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Changes currently selected item.

Changes the option selected in select widget. This is called by browser whenever user has chosen a different item. Most likely after calling this, a call to ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+popup\+\_\+destroy might be made in order to close the popup.

Enables/disables the fullscreen mode by javascript fullscreen A\+P\+I. The javascript A\+P\+I allows to request full screen mode, for more information see\+: \href{http://dvcs.w3.org/hg/fullscreen/raw-file/tip/Overview.html}{\tt http\+://dvcs.\+w3.\+org/hg/fullscreen/raw-\/file/tip/\+Overview.\+html}

Default value for javascript fullscreen A\+P\+I setting is {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E}.

Queries if hyperlink auditing is enabled.

Hyperlink auditing is used if a hyperlink created by an {\ttfamily a} or {\ttfamily area} element has a {\ttfamily ping} attribute. Please refer to the hyperlink auditing specification at \href{http://www.whatwg.org/specs/web-apps/current-work/#hyperlink-auditing}{\tt http\+://www.\+whatwg.\+org/specs/web-\/apps/current-\/work/\#hyperlink-\/auditing}. Hyperlink auditing is disabled by default.

{\em o} & view object to query if hyperlink auditing is enabled\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} if hyperlink auditing is enabled, {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a84e4ad49158357287094aafd78c0c115}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+enable\+\_\+hyperlink\+\_\+auditing\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+enable\+\_\+hyperlink\+\_\+auditing\+\_\+set}}

Enables/disables hyperlink auditing.

Hyperlink auditing is used if a hyperlink created by an {\ttfamily a} or {\ttfamily area} element has a {\ttfamily ping} attribute. Please refer to the hyperlink auditing specification at \href{http://www.whatwg.org/specs/web-apps/current-work/#hyperlink-auditing}{\tt http\+://www.\+whatwg.\+org/specs/web-\/apps/current-\/work/\#hyperlink-\/auditing}. Hyperlink auditing is disabled by default.

\item[{Eina\+\_\+\+Bool}]{enable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a2b3a9621d87af3646f8abeacdcce4984}
Enables/disables the X\+S\+S\+Auditor feature.

The X\+S\+S\+Auditor (cross-\/site scripting protection) feature provides protection from reflected X\+S\+S attacks on vulnerable web sites. When X\+S\+S is encountered in the page, frame sends a signal \char`\"{}xss,detected\char`\"{} with additional information on whether the entire page was blocked or only injected scripts were removed. This feature is enabled by default.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to set the X\+S\+S\+Auditor feature. \\
\hline
{\em enable} & {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} to enable the X\+S\+S\+Auditor feature, {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} to disable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_add6263687d73c65fce353a131d99f2cd}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+local\+\_\+storage\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+local\+\_\+storage\+\_\+set}}

\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+local\+\_\+storage\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+local\+\_\+storage\+\_\+set (

\item[{Eina\+\_\+\+Bool}]{enable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_add6263687d73c65fce353a131d99f2cd}
Enables/disables the local storage feature of H\+T\+M\+L5.

Please notice that by default there is no storage path specified for the database. This means that the contents of {\ttfamily window.\+local\+Storage} will not be saved to disk and will be lost when the view is removed. To set the path where the storage database will be stored, use ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+local\+\_\+storage\+\_\+database\+\_\+path\+\_\+set.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} on success or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_ae3115025b835f37cb99c49626e347d2c}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+private\+\_\+browsing\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+private\+\_\+browsing\+\_\+set}}

\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+private\+\_\+browsing\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+setting\+\_\+private\+\_\+browsing\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{Eina\+\_\+\+Bool}]{enable}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_ae3115025b835f37cb99c49626e347d2c}
Enables/disables the private browsing feature.

When this option is set, Web\+Core will avoid storing any record of browsing activity that may persist on disk or remain displayed when the option is reset.

This option does not affect the storage of such information in R\+A\+M.

The following functions respect this setting\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item H\+T\+M\+L5/\+D\+O\+M Storage
\item Icon Database
\item Console Messages
\item Memory\+Cache
\item Application Cache
\item Back/\+Forward Page History
\item Page Search Results
\item H\+T\+T\+P Cookies
\item Plug-\/ins (that support N\+P\+N\+Vprivate\+Mode\+Bool)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to set the private browsing feature \\
\hline
{\em enable} & {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} to enable the private browsing feature {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} to disable\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} on success or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets whether scripts are allowed to access clipboard.

The default value is {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E}. If set to {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E}, document.\+exec\+Command() allows cut, copy and paste commands.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} if the setting could be changed successfully, {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} in case an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets the smart class api, enabling view to be inherited.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em api} & class definition to set, all members with the exception of {\itshape Evas\+\_\+\+Smart\+\_\+\+Class-\/$>$data} may be overridden, must {\bfseries not} be {\ttfamily N\+U\+L\+L} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
{\itshape Evas\+\_\+\+Smart\+\_\+\+Class-\/$>$data} is used to implement type checking and is not supposed to be changed/overridden. If you need extra data for your smart class to work, just extend Ewk\+\_\+\+View\+\_\+\+Smart\+\_\+\+Class instead.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} on success or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure (probably version mismatch) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_a43eb449b174863fcb68dc8af63d85276}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+visibility\+\_\+state\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{{\bf Ewk\+\_\+\+Page\+\_\+\+Visibility\+\_\+\+State}}]{page\+\_\+visible\+\_\+state, }
\item[{Eina\+\_\+\+Bool}]{initial\+\_\+state}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_a43eb449b174863fcb68dc8af63d85276}
Sets the visibility state of the page.

This function let Web\+Kit knows the visibility status of the page. Web\+Kit will save the current status, and fire a \char`\"{}visibilitychange\char`\"{} event which web application can listen. Web application could slow down or stop itself when it gets a \char`\"{}visibilitychange\char`\"{} event and its visibility state is hidden. If its visibility state is visible, then the web application could use more resources.

This feature makes that web application could use the resources efficiently, such as power, C\+P\+U, and etc.

If more detailed description is needed, please see the specification. (\href{http://www.w3.org/TR/page-visibility}{\tt http\+://www.\+w3.\+org/\+T\+R/page-\/visibility})


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to set the visibility state. \\
\hline
{\em page\+\_\+visible\+\_\+state} & the visible state of the page to set. \\
\hline
{\em initial\+\_\+state} & {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} if this function is called at page initialization time, {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} on success or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_af09a738a3851d3e602bae9c81a39d113}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{float}]{zoom, }
\item[{float}]{duration, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{cx, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{cy}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_af09a738a3851d3e602bae9c81a39d113}
Sets the current zoom level while animating.

If the view was already animating to another zoom, it will start from current point to the next provided zoom ({\itshape zoom} parameter) and duration ({\itshape duration} parameter).

This is the recommended way to do transitions from one level to another. However, one may wish to do those from outside, in that case use \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_accc8e8cbdbbf53e5c7855190ab86b84d}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set()} and later control intermediate states with \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a25fef98c3856f87d8a74200efc5a1108}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+current()}, \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a2461f28c1cd7fbe0ec2d36a361bd5680}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+end()} and \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a09b47aa22a8d6933d2671ecc212e3a4a}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+stop()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to animate \\
\hline
{\em zoom} & final zoom level to use \\
\hline
{\em duration} & time in seconds the animation should take. \\
\hline
{\em cx} & offset inside object that defines zoom center. 0 is left side \\
\hline
{\em cy} & offset inside object that defines zoom center. 0 is top side \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} if animation will be started, {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} if not because zoom is too small/big 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_ad1337976086adeccfa21ca08363b7192}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+get@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+get}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_ad1337976086adeccfa21ca08363b7192}

\hypertarget{ewk__view_8h_accc8e8cbdbbf53e5c7855190ab86b84d}{\index{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}!ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set}}
\index{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set@{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set}!ewk\+\_\+view.\+h@{ewk\+\_\+view.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}E\+A\+P\+I Eina\+\_\+\+Bool ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+weak\+\_\+set (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Object $\ast$}]{o, }
\item[{float}]{zoom, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{cx, }
\item[{Evas\+\_\+\+Coord}]{cy}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{ewk__view_8h_accc8e8cbdbbf53e5c7855190ab86b84d}
Sets the current zoom level of backing store, centered at given point.

Unlike \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a2d7c9971c40b14dbb9eac1a66dcfa4e8}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+set()}, this call do not ask Web\+Kit to render at new size, but scale what is already rendered, being much faster but worse quality.

Often one should use \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_af09a738a3851d3e602bae9c81a39d113}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set()}, it will call the same machinery internally.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
this will set variables used by \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_af09a738a3851d3e602bae9c81a39d113}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+set()} so sub-\/classes will not reset internal state on their \char`\"{}calculate\char`\"{} phase. To unset those and enable sub-\/classes to reset their internal state, call \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a09b47aa22a8d6933d2671ecc212e3a4a}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+stop()}. Namely, this call will set \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a54fc660b30851f2e54f98d5fe0d59477}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+start()} to actual webkit zoom level, \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a2461f28c1cd7fbe0ec2d36a361bd5680}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+end()} and \hyperlink{ewk__view_8h_a25fef98c3856f87d8a74200efc5a1108}{ewk\+\_\+view\+\_\+zoom\+\_\+animated\+\_\+mark\+\_\+current()} to given zoom level.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em o} & view object to set the weak zoom level \\
\hline
{\em zoom} & a new level to scale backing store \\
\hline
{\em cx} & horizontal center offset, relative to object (w/2 is middle) \\
\hline
{\em cy} & vertical center offset, relative to object (h/2 is middle)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+T\+R\+U\+E} on success or {\ttfamily E\+I\+N\+A\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+S\+E} otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}
